# Keeper Documentation Portal

## Home

- [Keeper Documentation](https://docs.keeper.io/keeper-documentation.md): End-User Guides, Administrator Guides and Release Notes for All Keeper Products and Services

## User Guides

- [Keeper End-User Guides](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/readme.md): Guides for consumer and business end-users on desktop and mobile devices.
- [System Requirements](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/system-requirements.md): The system requirements for Keeper applications are listed below.
- [Quick Start Guides](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/quick-start-guides.md): The following Quick Start Guides will walk you through the setup steps and main features of Keeper for Web Vault & Desktop App, iOS, and Android.
- [Web Vault & Desktop App](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/quick-start-guides/quick-start-guide.md): This Quick Start Guide will walk you through the setup steps and main features of the Keeper Web Vault & Desktop App, linking additional resources throughout for more detailed instructions.
- [iOS - iPhone & iPad](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/quick-start-guides/ios-iphone-ipad.md): This Quick Start Guide will walk you through the set up steps and main features of the Keeper iOS App, linking additional resources throughout for more detailed instructions.
- [Android - Phone & Tablet](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/quick-start-guides/android.md): This Quick Start Guide will walk you through the setup steps and main features of Keeper's Android App, linking additional resources throughout for more detailed instructions.
- [Enterprise End-User](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/enterprise-end-user-setup-master-password.md): This end-user guide was created for Enterprise customers who login to Keeper using a Master Password.
- [Enterprise End-User (SSO)](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/enterprise-end-user-setup-sso.md): This end-user guide was created for Enterprise customers who deploy Keeper through an existing Single Sign-On Identity Provider (IdP) such as Azure, ADFS or Okta.
- [Web Vault & Desktop App](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/web-vault.md): A comprehensive guide for the Keeper Web Vault and cross-platform, Keeper Desktop Application.
- [Browser Extensions](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/browser-extensions.md): User guides for the KeeperFill Browser Extension for Chrome, Firefox, Safari, Microsoft Edge, Opera and other Chromium-based browsers.
- [Install for Chrome](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/browser-extensions/keeperfill-for-chrome-and-brave.md): Installation instructions for KeeperFill for Chrome, Brave and other Chromium-based browsers.
- [Install for Firefox](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/browser-extensions/keeperfill-for-firefox.md): Installation instructions for KeeperFill for Firefox.
- [Install for Safari](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/browser-extensions/keeperfill-for-safari.md): Installation and usage instructions for the KeeperFill extension on Safari.
- [Install for Edge](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/browser-extensions/keeperfill-for-edge.md): Installation instructions for KeeperFill for Edge.
- [Install for Opera](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/browser-extensions/keeperfill-for-opera.md): Installation instructions for KeeperFill for Opera.
- [Enterprise Deployment](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/browser-extensions/enterprise-deployment.md): Deploying the Browser Extension through group policy
- [KeeperFill for Apps](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/keeperfill-for-apps.md): This guide provides an overview of the main features of KeeperFill for Apps, a convenient tool used to enhance your experience using the Keeper Desktop App on Mac and Windows OS.
- [iOS - iPhone & iPad](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/ios.md): A comprehensive guide for Keeper for Apple iOS (iPhone, iPad) devices.
- [Autofill & Passkey Setup for iOS](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/autofill-setup-for-ios.md): Setup guide for Keeper's autofill & passkey features, KeeperFill for Apple iOS (iPhone, iPad) devices.
- [Android Phone & Tablet](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/android.md): Comprehensive guide for Keeper on Android phones and tablets.
- [Autofill & Passkey Setup for Android](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/autofill-setup-for-android.md): How to Set Up Autofill on Android
- [Record Types](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/record-types.md): How to create and manage new types of records in your vault
- [Sharing](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/sharing.md): With Keeper's powerful record sharing capabilities, users can securely share their records and folders with family, friends, co-workers and others across all devices, with ease.
- [Nested Share Subfolders](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/sharing/nested-share-subfolders.md): Coming Soon With Early Access Available by Request
- [Time-Limited Access](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/sharing/time-limited-access.md): Time-Limited Access allows you to securely share records and folders with other Keeper users on a temporary basis.
- [One-Time Share](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/sharing/one-time-share.md): Time-limited secure sharing of a record with anyone even if they don't have a Keeper account.
- [Self-Destructing Records](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/sharing/self-destructing-records.md): Self-Destructing Records allow you to share records with users outside of Keeper, while automatically deleting the record from your vault and disabling the share link at specified time.
- [Vault Offline Access](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/vault-offline-access.md): Offline access is a common use case for users who require vault access in poor network conditions.
- [Security Audit](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/security-audit.md): Security Audit provides password security strength reporting in your vault.
- [BreachWatch](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/breachwatch.md): User guide for BreachWatch on Keeper's Web Vault & Desktop App.
- [Secure File Storage](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/secure-file-storage.md): User guide for Keeper's Secure File Storage for Web Vault & Desktop App, iOS and Android.
- [Emergency Access](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/emergency-access.md): Give trusted family and friends access to your Keeper Vault.
- [Keeper Family Plan](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/keeper-family-plan.md): This guide provides an overview of Keeper's Family Plan, including how to sign up, invite family members and accept account invitations.
- [KeeperChat](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/keeperchat.md): This guide provides a look at the benefits and features of KeeperChat, Keeper's secure messaging solution.
- [Notification Center](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/notification-center.md): The notification center consolidates important in-app messages for the Keeper platform
- [Passkeys](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/passkeys.md): How to store and manage your passkeys with Keeper
- [Keeper Forcefield](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/keeper-forcefield.md): End-user guide for Keeper Forcefield - Windows Endpoint Protection for Sensitive Data
- [Troubleshooting](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/troubleshooting.md): This guide provides basic troubleshooting solutions to some of the more common questions users may have.
- [Reporting Autofill Issues](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/troubleshooting/autofill-issues.md): How to report autofill issues to Keeper
- [Troubleshoot Extension Issues](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/troubleshooting/troubleshooting-with-support.md): Steps to provide Keeper Support with Browser Extension debug information.
- [Troubleshooting Vault Issues](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/troubleshooting/troubleshooting-vault-issues.md): Troubleshooting instructions for troubleshooting vault issues.
- [Master Password Reset & Account Recovery](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/troubleshooting/reset-your-master-password.md): How to recover your Keeper account
- [Hardware Security Keys on Mobile](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/troubleshooting/hardware-security-keys-on-mobile.md): Support for FIDO2 security keys on Keeper for mobile devices.
- [Clearing Your Browser Cache](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/troubleshooting/clearing-browser-extension-cache.md): Clear the browser and extension cache to reset Keeper on your device using Keeper's browser extension tool.

- [Tips & Tricks](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/tips-and-tricks.md): This guide provides access to our top "tips & tricks" and assists users in optimizing their experience with Keeper on both desktop and mobile devices.

- [Stay Logged In](https://docs.keeper.io/user-guides/tips-and-tricks/stay-logged-in.md): This guide reviews how to enable the new Stay Logged In feature and extend your Logout Timer setting.

## Enterprise and MSP Guide

- [Keeper Enterprise and MSP Guide](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/readme.md): Keeper is the leading zero-trust and zero-knowledge identity security and Privileged Access Management (PAM) platform
- [Start Your Trial](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/start-free-trial.md): Creating a trial of Keeper Business and MSP
- [Keeper for Teams and Small Business](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/quick-start-guide-for-small-business-teams.md): This quick start guide will help get your small business team up and running with Keeper Business in just minutes
- [Keeper Enterprise](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/why-choose-keeper-enterprise.md): Keeper is a cybersecurity platform for preventing password-related data breaches and cyberthreats.
- [Subscriptions](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/subscriptions.md): Keeper's Subscriptions tab in the Admin Console gives eligible administrators the ability to manage, purchase, and upgrade their organization's Keeper licenses directly — without leaving the console.
- [Resources](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/resources.md): Resources for getting started with Keeper Business and Enterprise edition
- [Keeper Encryption and Security Model Details](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/keeper-encryption-model.md): The full details of Keeper’s encryption and security model are outlined below, with block diagrams, implementation details and additional resources.
- [Implementation Overview](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/implementation-overview.md): High level steps for successful rollout of Keeper Enterprise
- [On-Prem vs. Cloud](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/on-prem-vs.-cloud.md): Which components of Keeper are on-premise versus Cloud-based?
- [Domain Reservation](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/domain-reservation.md): Reserve the use of domains for privacy and security
- [Keeper Admin Console Overview](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/getting-started-with-keeper-admin-console.md): The Keeper Admin Console provides administrative controls, user onboarding, reporting and auditing.
- [Nodes and Organizational Structure](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/nodes-and-organizational-structure.md): Keeper's node architecture scales for organizations of all sizes
- [User Management and Lifecycle](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-management-and-lifecycle.md): Managing users and lifecycles in the Keeper Admin Console
- [User and Team Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning.md): User provisioning is flexible and powerful with Keeper Enterprise
- [Custom Invite and Logo](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/custom-invite-and-logo.md): Configure a custom invite email and logo before inviting users
- [Custom Email - Markdown Language](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/custom-invite-and-logo/custom-email-markdown-language.md)
- [Simple Provisioning through the Admin Console](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/manual-provisioning-through-admin-console.md): Provision users and create teams from the Keeper Admin Console.
- [Active Directory Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/syncing-active-directory-or-ldap.md): Keeper AD Bridge supports automatic provisioning of nodes, roles, teams and users across any size Active Directory environment.
- [LDAP Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/ldap-provisioning.md): Keeper AD Bridge supports automatic provisioning of nodes, roles, teams and users from any LDAP service.
- [SSO JIT (Just-in-Time) Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/single-sign-on-saml-2.0-authentication.md): Keeper supports just-in-time automatic provisioning and seamless authentication with any identity provider
- [API Provisioning with SCIM](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/automated-provisioning-with-scim.md): Keeper supports direct SCIM API provisioning for any 3rd party identity provider
- [Using SCIM API Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/automated-provisioning-with-scim/using-scim-api-provisioning.md): This page contains information on how to use Postman, a popular API platform to provision your users into your Keeper tenant.
- [Okta Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/okta-integration-with-saml-and-scim.md): Keeper supports SAML 2.0 Authentication and SCIM provisioning with the Okta platform.
- [Entra ID / Azure AD Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/azure-ad-provisioning-scim.md): Keeper supports SAML 2.0 Authentication and SCIM provisioning with the Azure AD / Entra ID platform.
- [Google Workspace Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/google-g-suite-scim.md): Keeper supports SAML 2.0 Authentication and SCIM provisioning with the Google Workspace platform.
- [JumpCloud Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/jumpcloud-provisioning-with-scim.md): Keeper supports SAML 2.0 Authentication and SCIM provisioning with JumpCloud
- [CloudGate Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/cloudgate-provisioning-with-scim.md): Keeper supports SAML 2.0 Authentication and SCIM provisioning with CloudGate UNO
- [OneLogin Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/onelogin-provisioning-with-scim.md): Keeper supports SAML 2.0 Authentication and SCIM provisioning with the OneLogin platform.
- [Microsoft AD FS Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/microsoft-adfs.md): Keeper supports SAML 2.0 Authentication and SCIM provisioning with Microsoft AD FS
- [Team and User Approvals](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/approval-queue.md): Manual and Automated approval of SCIM or Bridge-provisioned Users & Teams
- [Email Auto-Provisioning](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/email-auto-provisioning.md): Basic provisioning of users based on email address
- [CLI Provisioning with Commander SDK](https://docs.keeper.io/enterprise-guide/user-and-team-provisioning/cli-provisioning-with-commander-sdk.md): Keeper Commander is an open-source Python SDK which can perform many vault and administrative functions within the Keeper system.

# Agent Instructions: Querying This Documentation

If you need additional information, you can query the documentation dynamically by asking a question.

Perform an HTTP GET request on a page URL with the `ask` query parameter:

```
GET https://docs.keeper.io/keeper-documentation.md?ask=<question>
```

The question should be specific, self-contained, and written in natural language.
The response will contain a direct answer to the question and relevant excerpts and sources from the documentation.

Use this mechanism when the answer is not explicitly present in the current page, you need clarification or additional context, or you want to retrieve related documentation sections.
